<div id="review_578842499" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/578842499" />
    <a title="Lori McD" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5878249-lori-mcd"><img alt="Lori McD" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1370647477p2/5878249.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/578842499?book_show_action=true">Apr 02, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lori McD" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lori McD" href="/user/show/5878249-lori-mcd">Lori McD</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was ok"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was ok</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/17339217-fever">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=guilty-pleasure">guilty-pleasure</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=kindle-book">kindle-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=series">series</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=steamy">steamy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=chick-lit">chick-lit</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=tough-subject-matter">tough-subject-matter</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=social-issues">social-issues</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5878249-lori-mcd?shelf=own">own</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer578842499" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1921800798226017066">2.5, maybe 3 stars<br/><br/>From the other reviews, I'm in the minority here. I'm not gushing over this book. Yeah... I really wanted to like this book, and it was a decent read. But it didn't GRAB me like Maya's and Gabe's story did in book 1. It's not a bad book... it probably deserves a 3 star rating, because I *did* read it, and I *generally* liked it. I just didn't feel the chemistry between Bethany and Jace, despite his obsession with her. It really did seem too much like a cross between Pretty Woma</span>
  <span id="freeText1921800798226017066" style="display:none">2.5, maybe 3 stars<br /><br />From the other reviews, I'm in the minority here. I'm not gushing over this book. Yeah... I really wanted to like this book, and it was a decent read. But it didn't GRAB me like Maya's and Gabe's story did in book 1. It's not a bad book... it probably deserves a 3 star rating, because I *did* read it, and I *generally* liked it. I just didn't feel the chemistry between Bethany and Jace, despite his obsession with her. It really did seem too much like a cross between Pretty Woman and FSOG (with a whole better setup and better, stronger characters).<br /><br />And, unfortunately, this story is completely predictable in almost every way. Sure, I want to find out what happens to them all from here, especially Jack. But was I one bit surprised at what happened? No. The story is fairly well-written and definitely has it's moments, but I didn't feel the *need* to read it to know how it would end.<br /><br />Bethany's lived a hard life, and I empathized with her, even her insecurities. I guess that for someone who's lived on the streets most of her life, this whole scenario would be more than a little overwhelming. While I can see how she'd appreciate Jace's 24/7 almost TPE (total power exchange) - taking almost complete control of her life, giving her a schedule, deciding what she wears and eats, when they have sex, etc. - after awhile, I can also see her rebelling. And because of the way that they've started, will they have built enough trust and love together that Jace will stand by his assertions that he'll take her any way he can get her. 'Cuz in future, I see her being much more independent. It's one thing to allow Jace total control/dominance in the BDSM way in the bedroom and another to allow that same total control/dominance in her everyday waking life.<br /><br />I guess that's the catch: Bethany's life truly has been SO DIFFERENT from Jace, Gabe, Mia, and Ash, that despite how wonderful and accepting and loving these people are, they don't KNOW what it's been like for her. To go from wondering where your next meal is coming from and whether you'll have somewhere warm to sleep tonight to literally anything her heart desires and total protection and control from a man obsessed with her... well, that's going from 1 to 10 in .5 seconds. That's the part of the book that doesn't fit. Doesn't seem real.<br /><br />IF Bethany had a fairly normal upbringing but then something happened and she was out on the street surviving, OK. I could accept it. But that's not the case.<br /><br />And the whole thing with Jack. OK, he's not the best person to be around her. OK, he's got his own issues. But living as Bethany has for so long, the fact that Jace can't see or understand what Jack is to her... the fact that he's so threatened by Jack... well, it says a LOT about Jace and how he's relating to Bethany.<br /><br />To be fair, Ms. Banks TRIES to bring those elements in. But most of it gets lost in the HEA of the romance genre. The harsher edges are smoothed down by appeasing the reader with mild BDSM scenes. Yes, Bethany's realization about TRUST and Jace is very good - very real. But it's not really addressed, front-and-center; it's acknowledged, barely discussed, and then swept under the rug in favor of Jace's determination to be forever with Bethany and provide everything and anything she could ever want.<br /><br />The way that Jace and even Ash talks most of the time, without a subject - "Wanna blahblahblah..." "Have to thisorthat..." - drove me crazy after awhile. It was totally overdone. No one talks that way all the time.<br /><br />So... I have a lot of mixed feelings about this one. I'm hoping that Ash's story is more in line with some sort of reality.<br /><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="1921800798226017066" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_523602276" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/523602276" />
    <a title="Lady Allison" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2802505-lady-allison"><img alt="Lady Allison" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1387596480p2/2802505.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/523602276?book_show_action=true">Feb 01, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Lady Allison" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Lady Allison" href="/user/show/2802505-lady-allison">Lady Allison</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="did not like it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">did not like it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2802505-lady-allison?shelf=red-hot-books">red-hot-books</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer523602276" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10276097549252498872"><b>This review & others also found on <a href='http://www.redhotbooks.com/2013/04/review-fever.html' rel='nofollow noopener'>Red Hot Books</a></b><br/><br/>Let me preface my review by saying that I loved Ms. Banks' Sweet series. I think she's a talented writer and I have always enjoyed reading the relationships she creates. That being said, this book was hard to get through.<br/><br/>This is the second book in the Breathless series, the story of Jace Crestwell and Bethany Willis. Jace is a self made millionaire who sees Bethany at his sister's engagement party from across the room and wants her immediately. Bet</span>
  <span id="freeText10276097549252498872" style="display:none"><b>This review &amp; others also found on <a href="http://www.redhotbooks.com/2013/04/review-fever.html" rel="nofollow noopener">Red Hot Books</a></b><br /><br />Let me preface my review by saying that I loved Ms. Banks' Sweet series. I think she's a talented writer and I have always enjoyed reading the relationships she creates. That being said, this book was hard to get through.<br /><br />This is the second book in the Breathless series, the story of Jace Crestwell and Bethany Willis. Jace is a self made millionaire who sees Bethany at his sister's engagement party from across the room and wants her immediately. Bethany is a homeless woman forced to do odd jobs to keep money in her pocket, since no one will hire her on a continuous basis. When Bethany is confronted by Ash, Jace's best friend and the man he shares his women with, what she sees for the evening is a guaranteed place to sleep and a warm meal for free. She agrees to go upstairs with them both, even though Jace doesn't seem 100% on board. After they spend the night together, Jace wakes up to find Bethany gone and goes crazy. He spends two weeks tracking her down and eventually finds her in a women's shelter and steals her away. <br /><br />This story is very unique in that I've never read about a homeless heroine, and it was very interesting to get inside her mind and watch her face situations most people don't have to. However, I was less than impressed with Jace. He completely took over Bethany's life without thought to how she might feel about it. Granted, she didn't have much of a life to live, but for me, a woman's choice is one of the most important things she has to hold on to. Which brings to me to my biggest issue with this story. <br /><br />I understand that there is a delicate balance between building trust and taking care of the person you love while being the dominant partner in the relationship. However, I felt that the dominance went over board. Jace was more than just "demanding" or "exacting". He was a pushy jerk. <br /><br /><i>"Do you understand that I would be in absolute control over every aspect of our relationship, Bethany? Do you really get that? That every decision will be made by me. Where we eat, what we eat, where we go, where you go. When we have sex. When we don't have sex. What you wear. Who you talk to. Are you getting it yet? I'm a controlling bastard and that won't change. Are you really willing to sign on for something like that?"</i><br /><br />I don't mind a man taking care of me or not having to think about things for a while, but since when did becoming an all out asshat become a good thing in a hero? He crossed the line so many times it was hard to count. <br /><br /><i>As soon as Jace had taken that step in exerting his dominance, a part of her had sighed in relief. It had been so freeing to hand over responsibility to someone who cared about her. Someone who took care of her and was insanely protective of her. It gave her a measure of security she hadn't enjoyed until now. It made her feel... safe.</i><br /><br />How can I argue with that? If that's what it took to make her feel safe, who am I to judge? It's just not my thing. My mind rebelled the whole way through. I liked Bethany a lot, even when her constant self hatred got tiring, I wanted her to have a better life and a better future. <br /><br />In the end, I think this may simply be a case of "not my cup of tea" - but it may be yours, who knows? Either way, it's a breathtaking cover; I still enjoy the author, but I won't be following up with this series. <br /><br />Grade: D<br /><br /><i>*ARC Provided by Berkley</i></span>

<div id="review_599895100" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/599895100" />
    <a title="Didi" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/6082482-didi"><img alt="Didi" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1459297426p2/6082482.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/599895100?book_show_action=true">Apr 25, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Didi" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Didi" href="/user/show/6082482-didi">Didi</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=betrayal">betrayal</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=adult-contemporary-romance">adult-contemporary-romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=billionairre-alpha-male">billionairre-alpha-male</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6082482-didi?shelf=insta-love">insta-love</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer599895100" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9131623808524976790">********** 3 - 3.5 STARS **********<br/><br/>The second book in Banks' Breathless trilogy was good, though not as good as the first one IMO. This time around we're given the story of Jace and Bethany, a down on her luck homeless woman swept up in an instant and electrifying romance with the billionnaire.<br/><br/>I liked the pacing of this book and have to say that although it didn't wow me as much as the first, Maya Banks writes romance extremely well. It was easy to be caught up in it and I found myself finishing</span>
  <span id="freeText9131623808524976790" style="display:none">********** 3 - 3.5 STARS **********<br /><br />The second book in Banks' Breathless trilogy was good, though not as good as the first one IMO. This time around we're given the story of Jace and Bethany, a down on her luck homeless woman swept up in an instant and electrifying romance with the billionnaire.<br /><br />I liked the pacing of this book and have to say that although it didn't wow me as much as the first, Maya Banks writes romance extremely well. It was easy to be caught up in it and I found myself finishing it faster because of that.<br /><br />I like Gabe. I liked Jace. But I LOVE ASH! If I'm being honest, I read this partly for the story and largely for glimpses of the enticing Ash McIntyre. He melted me in Rush, even with his limited story time and although I didn't see as much as I would have of him in Fever, the scenes involving him made me want him more. Obviously I can't wait to read Burn!<br /><br />Back to Jace and Bethany. They were very sweet and cute together. Jace was, like his brethern, the dominating alpha male turned soft by the love of the right woman. He was tender and wonderful even when he was angry. And while I liked Bethany, I liked Mia a lot more. Bethany was sweet and deserved her life to change at the hands of a man that would cherish her but I just couldn't connect with her at all. Her naivety annoyed me sometimes but really I didn't empathize with her like I did Mia.<br /><br />Regardless of all that this book, like it's forerunner, was great to read. The chapters aren't excessively long which adds to the pacing and Maya Banks manages to instill interest in the vaguest of occurrences. Its also nice to read about men that have earned their wealth, at a realistic age, rather than the unlikely occurrence of being a billionaire in their twenties. I'm off to read Burn and finally get Ash all to myself!<br /><br />GENRE: Contemporary Romance<br />STEAM: High with light BDSM<br />POV: 3rd person<br />CLIFFY: HEA with Burn being Ash's story</span>
  <a data-text-id="9131623808524976790" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

  <span id="freeText16528559600793116500" style="display:none"><b>RATING AROUND 3 - 3.5 STARS </b><br><br><br><i>I'm feeling 50/50 about this one. I don't hate it, I don't love it either.</i><br><br><i>
  <b>Me while reading the book:</b>
</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793191.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793192.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793193.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793194.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793195.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793196.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793197.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793198.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793199.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1380406518ra/793200.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><br>Yep. That pretty much sums it up. First few pages were really interesting. But then as you go along, the story kinda drags you.... The good thing about it is that our hero, Jace Crestwell, is one sexy beast!!! I love him. He's my favorite out of the 3 musketeers. He's sexy, uber alpha, domineering, possessive, sweet, loving, tender, passionate, a very crazy SOB but he is still just PERFECT!<br><br><blockquote>
  <i>“I’m real, baby. This is real. We are real. The sooner you accept that, the sooner we can move forward and you can be happy. I want you to be happy. I want you to be content. Warm. For you not to have to worry about your next meal. Most of all, I want you to know without a doubt that I’ve got your back. And your front. And your sides. I’ve got all of you and I’m not letting go.”<br><br>“All I know is that when I looked across the room that night at the party and saw you, everything changed for me. There was instant recognition. No, I didn’t know anything about you at that point, but what I did know was that you were going to be mine. As for that bullshit about me not wanting you after you told me about your past, well, it’s just that. Bullshit. We all make mistakes, baby. Nobody is perfect. I’m not. You’re not. It would be boring as shit if we were.”<br><br>“I’m not saying this is going to be easy. I’ll make mistakes. You’ll make mistakes—mostly about trying to draw attention to the differences between us. I realize it’ll take time for you to get over this mind-set that you’re somehow not good enough for me. It pisses me off but I get that you can’t change a lifetime of seeing yourself the way you do overnight. But I’m going to work on it and I’m going to wear you down, so just be forewarned. I’m a persistent bastard and I never walk away from<br>something I want, whether in business or my personal life.”<br></i>
</blockquote><br><br>See? He always say the right words. Such a dreamy man. <br><br>So yes, I'm kind of disappointed with the series. Maybe because I expected too much from the author? I didn't really like the first book as well (<i>although I think I gave it 3 or 4 stars because of Gabe</i>), just because it has the same problems with this one. Before it came out I was soooo intrigued and curious with the series because the blurb was pretty awesome.... But oh well. <br><br>I am still going to read the last one on the series and I hope the third would be as awesome as pancakes. <br><br><br><br></span>
  <a data-text-id="16528559600793116500" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

Five stars. <br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392087161ra/8498512.gif' width='' height='' alt='' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This was amazing. Bethany is so cute! She had a horrible life :( until she met Jace :)<br/>It’s the first time I could understand the real meaning of this kind of relationship.   <span id="freeText6751858456095218980" style="display:none">Fuck it. Five stars. <br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1392087161ra/8498512.gif" width="" height="" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This was amazing. Bethany is so cute! She had a horrible life :( until she met Jace :)<br>It’s the first time I could understand the real meaning of this kind of relationship. They made me understand everything!<br><br><i>“The kind of power you’re talking about isn’t about control. It isn’t about your submission. It isn’t about my dominance. It’s about emotional power. But baby, you have exactly that same power over me. When it comes to our relationship, you have far more power than I do.”<br>Her eyes widened in surprise.<br>“It’s true,” he said before she could put her protest to words. “You have more power, more control than you could possibly imagine. My heart is in your hands. That’s not bullshit. I’m not saying stuff I think you want to hear in order to manipulate you. I can’t be any more honest than this. I’m yours, baby. I’m putting it out there. My heart, my soul, it all belongs to you.”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420771266ra/13259868.gif" width="" height="" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Promise me that if it’s ever too much, if you’re ever overwhelmed, if I ever push too hard or too fast, that you’ll tell me. I never want to make you feel bad about what we do.”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420771266ra/13259869.gif" width="" height="" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><i>“Do you understand that I would be in absolute control over every aspect of our relationship, Bethany? Are you getting it yet? I’m a controlling bastard and that won’t change. Are you really willing to sign on for something like that?”<br>“And if I’m not?” she asked, studying him every bit as intently as he studied her.<br>“Then I’ll accept whatever you can give me,” he said quietly.<br>She sucked in her breath until she was light-headed. Oh my God. After all he’d said. After all he’d explained. He’d push down all that made him who he was just to have her.</i><br><br>This moment was lovely. He didn’t lie to her. He didn’t play any tricks. He explained her well. I like him. <s>I love him, actually.</s><br><br><i>“Will you wear my collar, Bethany? It’s not only a symbol of my possession. It’s a symbol of your gift to me but also my gift to you. I will absolutely cherish and protect you. See that your every need is met. Your body will be mine, but mine will also be yours. I will love and adore you with everything that is me.”</i><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1420771266ra/13259870.gif" width="" height="" alt="" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

<div id="review_582370430" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/582370430" />
    <a title="Elyse" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/231347-elyse"><img alt="Elyse" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1496673928p2/231347.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/582370430?book_show_action=true">Apr 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Elyse" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Elyse" href="/user/show/231347-elyse">Elyse</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>



        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer582370430" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17910138436334380139">I enjoyed this book but not nearly as much as Rush. I didn't feel the chemistry between Jace and Bethany that I did with Gabe and Mia.<br/><br/>When Jace meets Bethany it's love at first sight. They have a one-night stand (one night three-way?) with his friend Ash, with whom he has always shared women. Jace realizes immediately that he wants Bethany to himself. When he wakes up the next morning she's gone.<br/><br/>Jace tracks Bethany down, but finds that she's homeless. He immediately rescues her, providing her wi</span>
  <span id="freeText17910138436334380139" style="display:none">I enjoyed this book but not nearly as much as Rush. I didn't feel the chemistry between Jace and Bethany that I did with Gabe and Mia.<br /><br />When Jace meets Bethany it's love at first sight. They have a one-night stand (one night three-way?) with his friend Ash, with whom he has always shared women. Jace realizes immediately that he wants Bethany to himself. When he wakes up the next morning she's gone.<br /><br />Jace tracks Bethany down, but finds that she's homeless. He immediately rescues her, providing her with clothing, an apartment, etc. I know this was supposed to be a Cinderella story, but I couldn't get over Bethany's homelessness. I felt it impacted how I read their relationship.<br /><br />Bethany makes it clear she loves Jace and wants to be with him, but part of me kept thinking--yeah and the alternative would be what? Go back to the women's shelter.<br /><br />Also I didn't connect with Jace. He's tempermental and demanding, but it's never explained why. His constant swearing actually got repetitive after awhile.<br /><br />I still enjoyed this book and finished it in two days, but since Rush totally knocked my socks off, it was a little bit of a let down.</span>
  <a data-text-id="17910138436334380139" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

//<![CDATA[  

  function submitShelfLink(unique_id, book_id, shelf_id, shelf_name, submit_form, exclusive) {
    var checkbox_id = 'shelf_name_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    var element = document.getElementById(checkbox_id)

    var checked = element.checked
    if (checked && exclusive) {
      // can't uncheck a radio by clicking it!
      return
    }
    if(document.getElementById("savingMessage")){
      Element.show('savingMessage')
    }
    var element_id = 'shelfInDropdownName_' + unique_id + '_' + shelf_id;
    Element.update(element_id, "saving...");
    if (submit_form) {
      Element.hide('shelfDropdown_' + unique_id)
      var form = document.getElementById('addBookForm' + book_id)
      if (form) {
        form.shelf.value = shelf_name
        form.onsubmit()
      }
    }
    else {
      var action = checked ? 'remove' : ''
      element.checked = !element.checked
      new Ajax.Request('/shelf/add_to_shelf', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name)}, parameters:'book_id=' + book_id + '&name=' + shelf_name + '&a=' + action + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('MMveY/2CZg3Aor090nWJuqpIW/wHS0nE2WFW/P9xuKPeg8NVgyXGfYOPUu3704aK+0Y+YJEzk4izbOF7ijiVKw==')})
    }
  }

  function shelfSubmitted(request, book_id, checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name) {
    Element.update('shelfListfalse_' + book_id, request.responseText)
    afterShelfSave(checkbox_id, element_id, unique_id, shelf_name.escapeHTML())
  }

  function refreshGroupBox(group_id, book_id) {
    new Ajax.Updater('addGroupBooks' + book_id + '', '/group/add_book_box', {asynchronous:true, evalScripts:true, onSuccess:function(request){refreshGroupBoxComplete(request, book_id);}, parameters:'id=' + group_id + '&book_id=' + book_id + '&refresh=true' + '&authenticity_token=' + encodeURIComponent('/7A5G8Yfq2RQI+j2KUm72qiicItf0J43/oULxmp/ge8R+CQtuLgLFBMOByYA77Tq+awVF8moRHuUiLxBHzasZw==')})
  }
